  <script>
    var onImageLoad = function(event) {
      if (!window.pwtTempStorage) {
        window.pwtTempStorage = {};
      }

      var tgt = event.target;
      var dataImagePrefix = 'data:image';
      if (tgt.tagName === 'IMG' && tgt.parentElement && tgt.parentElement.dataset &&
        tgt.parentElement.dataset.pwt === 'true') {
        var key = tgt.src && tgt.src.substr(0, dataImagePrefix.length) === dataImagePrefix ?
          tgt.src : tgt.src.split('/').pop();
        if (!window.pwtTempStorage[key]) {
          window.pwtTempStorage[key] = {
            time: window.performance.now(),
            visibility: window.getComputedStyle(tgt).visibility,
          };
        }
      }
    }

    var calculateNumOfServerRenderedPinImages = function(event) {
      window.numOfServerRenderedPinImages = document.querySelectorAll('[data-pwt]').length;
    }

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", calculateNumOfServerRenderedPinImages);
    document.body.addEventListener('load', onImageLoad, true);

    window.addEventListener('load', function() {
      document.body.removeEventListener('load', onImageLoad, true);
      document.removeEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', calculateNumOfServerRenderedPinImages);
    });
  </script>

// search redirect
jQuery(document).ready(function() {
jQuery('#gcustom-search-form').submit(function(event) {
	var searchValue = jQuery('#edit-searchfield').val();
	event.preventDefault();
	window.location.href = "http://www.ooyala.com/search2?query="+searchValue;
});

// set no conflict mode for jQuery
var $jQ = jQuery.noConflict();

//Function to retrieve get parameters
function jsGet( name )
{
    name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
    var regexS = "[\\?&]"+name+"=([^&#]*)";
    var regex = new RegExp( regexS );
    var results = regex.exec( window.location.href );
    if( results == null )
       return "";
    else
       return results[1];
}


//Function to set Cookies for UTMS
function setUTMCookie(c_name,value,exdays, domain)
{
   var exdate=new Date();
   exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
   var c_value=escape(value) + ((exdays==null) ? "" : "; expires="+exdate.toUTCString());
   document.cookie=c_name + "=" + c_value + ( ( domain ) ? ";domain=" + domain : "" );
}


//Function to read UTM cookies
function getUTMCookie(c_name)
{
   var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");
   for (i=0;i<ARRcookies.length;i++)
   {
 	x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
 	y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);
 	x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
 	if (x==c_name)
        {
   	   return unescape(y);
        }
    }
}


(function ($) {

   $('form').submit(function(){
      setUTMCookie('form_submitted', '1', 365, 'ooyala.com');
     console.log($(this).serialize());
	});

  setTimeout(function(){

     //Check for the UTM parameters to set the new corresponding cookies
     if (jsGet('utm_source') && jsGet('utm_medium') && jsGet('utm_campaign')){
        var c = jsGet('utm_source')+';|'+jsGet('utm_medium')+';|'+jsGet('utm_campaign');
        setUTMCookie('ga_campaign_salesforce', c, 90, 'ooyala.com');
     }

     if (jsGet('utm_content')) {
        setUTMCookie('ga_utm_content', jsGet('utm_content'), 90, 'ooyala.com');
     }

     if (jsGet('utm_term')){
        setUTMCookie('ga_utm_term', jsGet('utm_term'), 90, 'ooyala.com');
     }

     //Check if the cookies currently exist or if it has been updated
     //to update the data in marketo after submission
     if( getUTMCookie("ga_utm_content") ){
        $("input[name=UTM_Content__c]").val( getUTMCookie("ga_utm_content") );
     }

     if (getUTMCookie("ga_utm_term")) {
        $("input[name=UTM_Term__c]").val( getUTMCookie("ga_utm_term") );
     }

     if (getUTMCookie("ga_campaign_salesforce")) {

        var utms=getUTMCookie("ga_campaign_salesforce");

        $("input[name=Web_Tracking_Campaign__c]").val( utms );


        var csplit = utms.indexOf(';|') != -1 ? ';|' : '-';

        utms = utms.split(csplit);

        $("input[name=UTM_Source__c]").val( utms[0] );
        $("input[name=UTM_Medium__c]").val( utms[1] );
        $("input[name=UTM_Name__c]").val( utms[2] );
     }
   }, 1000);

}($jQ));

<div id='lpeCDiv_93865' class='lpeCElement main'><span class='lpContentsItem richTextSpan'><h2>The Ooyala Q4 2016 Global Video Index has the latest on viewing habits around the globe</h2>

<p>Ever wonder how video viewing habits differ from region to region?</p>

<p>Ooyalas <strong>Q4 2016 Global Video Index</strong> has the details only Ooyala can provide: where long-form tablet viewing is most popular (think Latin America), who watches the most video on mobile (EMEA is leading the pack, but barely), and much more.</p>

<p>The Q4 2016 Video Index also has inside data on advertising, theater-vs-video trends (video is winning), and much more. Get the numbers you need as only Ooyala can deliver them: download the <strong>Q4 2016 Global Video Index</strong>.</p></span></div>
